[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA dynamic stack buffer overflow was detected during fuzz testing of the AVIF image [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconversion routines. The error arises when converting YUV image data to RGB in the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction `avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min reformat.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. AddressSanitizer reports an[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout-of-bounds [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte read from a stack-allocated buffer.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  While running the `YuvRgbFuzzTest.Convert` fuzz test under libFuzzer and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer, the code in `avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` attempts to read past [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe end of a stack buffer. The sanitizer report shows a READ of size [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m beyond a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleft alloca redzone. The failure stack trace leads from [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` through higher-level functions [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`avifImageYUVToRGBImpl`, `avifImageYUVToRGB`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and into the fuzz test harness in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`avif_fuzztest_yuvrgb.cc`.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is a stack-based buffer overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdynamic stack buffer overflow[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that can [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlead to memory corruption, crashes, or potentially arbitrary code execution.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations and findings  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The failure is reproducible under libFuzzer with `-[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m` on an existing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseed corpus entry.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • AddressSanitizer pinpoints the exact read location at reformat.c line [0m[1;36m812[0m[39m.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The call chain involves chroma conversion and rounding logic, suggesting the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow may stem from wrong assumptions about buffer sizing or stride.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash consistently occurs in the slow path [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot the fast path or optimized routines.[0m                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39maround line [0m[1;36m812[0m[39m—verify stack buffer allocations, indexing logic, and boundary [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m* [0m[1;36m1.[0m[39m0f[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;39m([0m[39mkg * Y[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[35m/[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m*kr*[0m[1;39m([0m[39mkr-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m738[0m[39m:                    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mG0Cr < G1Cr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m739[0m[39m:                        minCr = [0m[1;35mfmax[0m[1;39m([0m[39mminCr,G0Cr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m740[0m[39m:                        maxCr = [0m[1;35mfmin[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCr,G1Cr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m741[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m742[0m[39m:                        minCr = [0m[1;35mfmax[0m[1;39m([0m[39mminCr,G1Cr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m743[0m[39m:                        maxCr = [0m[1;35mfmin[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCr,G0Cr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m744[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m745[0m[39m:                    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m same for Cb[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m746[0m[39m:                    G0Cb = [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mkg*Y[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m+[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m*kr*kr*clampedCr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m-[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m*kr*clampedCr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[35m/[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m*[0m[1;39m([0m[39mkb-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m*kb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m747[0m[39m:                    G1Cb = [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mkg* [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m * [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mY[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m+kg-[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m*[0m[1;39m([0m[39mkr-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m*kr*clampedCr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[35m/[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[39m*[0m[1;39m([0m[39mkb-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m*kb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m749[0m[39m:                    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mG0Cb < G1Cb[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m750[0m[39m:                        minCb = [0m[1;35mfmax[0m[1;39m([0m[39mminCb,G0Cb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m751[0m[39m:                        maxCb = [0m[1;35mfmin[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCb,G1Cb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m752[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m753[0m[39m:                        minCb = [0m[1;35mfmax[0m[1;39m([0m[39mminCb,G1Cb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m754[0m[39m:                        maxCb = [0m[1;35mfmin[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCb,G0Cb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m755[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m756[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m757[0m[39m:                    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m check if the max somehow got lower than the min [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcan [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhappen if Y' = [0m[1;36m0.[0m[39m0f[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m758[0m[39m:                    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCr < minCr[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m759[0m[39m:                        float t = maxCr;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m760[0m[39m:                        maxCr = minCr;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m761[0m[39m:                        minCr = t;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m762[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m763[0m[39m:                    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmaxCb < minCb[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m764[0m[39m:                        float t = maxCb;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m765[0m[39m:                        maxCb = minCb;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m766[0m[39m:                        minCb = t;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m767[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m768[0m[39m:                    [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m769[0m[39m:                    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m sanity check clamp the spill[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m770[0m[39m:                    spill_Cr = [0m[1;35mAVIF_CLAMP[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCr - [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mAVIF_CLAMP[0m[1;39m([0m[39mCr,minCr,maxCr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m0.[0m[39m0f,[0m[1;36m1.[0m[39m0f[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/reformat.[0m[1;92mc:773[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m781[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m773[0m[39m:                    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m now we have generated the spill, get it's neigbors[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m774[0m[39m:                    int adjCol = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi%[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m775[0m[39m:                    int adjRow = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj%[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m776[0m[39m:                    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m check the bounds[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m777[0m[39m:                    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi + adjCol >= image->width[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m778[0m[39m:                        adjCol = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m779[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m780[0m[39m:                    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj + adjRow >= image->height[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m781[0m[39m:                        adjRow = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/reformat.[0m[1;92mc:810[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m818[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m810[0m[39m:                        uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m811[0m[39m:                        vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m812[0m[39m:                        uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m813[0m[39m:                        vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m814[0m[39m:                        uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m815[0m[39m:                        vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m816[0m[39m:                        uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m817[0m[39m:                        vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m818[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m   [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In the slow‐path function `avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreformat.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“dampening” code [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m812[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m recomputes two offsets `a` and `b` based solely [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mon pixel parity, then immediately indexes into the stack‐allocated arrays  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     float uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mwidth[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mheight[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     float vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mwidth[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mheight[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   without verifying that `i+a` and `j+b` remain within valid bounds. When `i` or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`j` sits at the right or bottom border and parity yields a +[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m offset, the code [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreads/writes past the end of these arrays, triggering a [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdynamic‐stack‐buffer‐overflow.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Strategy  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In the dampening block [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtotal_spill > [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` section[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, replace the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting `int a, b; if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m …[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` logic with boundary‐checked offsets.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Compute offsets exactly once:  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       int a = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi % [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       int b = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj % [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Immediately clamp each offset to zero if it would step out of range:  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mi + a < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mi + a >= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mimage->width[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  a = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mj + b < [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mj + b >= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mimage->height[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m b = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Use the clamped `a` and `b` for all neighbor adjustments:  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       - Always apply the self‐pixel dampening:  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       - If `a != [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`, adjust `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       - If `b != [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m`, adjust `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       - If both `a` and `b` are nonzero, adjust `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Why This Fix Is Correct  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It directly addresses the out‐of‐bounds reads/writes by ensuring every [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomputed index into the local 2D arrays remains within `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m..width-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m x [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m..height-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It preserves the existing spill‐and‐dampening algorithm for interior pixels, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monly disabling neighbor dampening at edges where it would overflow.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It does not alter any fuzzing harness, test code, utility API, or other [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconversion paths—only the slow‐path chroma “spill” routine in `reformat.c`.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The change is minimal and localized, so it avoids unintended interactions with[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mother functionality.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Edges of the image will receive less dampening [0m[1;39m([0m[39mneighbors effectively clamped [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto the pixel itself[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, but this mirrors the spill block’s existing behavior when [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbordering out‐of‐bounds.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No performance regression for large images [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe extra integer comparisons are [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnegligible compared to the floating‐point work[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding YuvRgbFuzzTest.Convert[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will continue to run under [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same harness without modification.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Steps to Implement  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `src/reformat.c` and locate the dampening block in [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` around the reported overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnear line [0m[1;36m812[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Replace lines defining `int a, b;` and their subsequent parity‐based [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39massignments with the boundary‐checked version described above.  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Replace each direct neighbor access [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39m…[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m…[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with guarded accesses that use the clamped `a` and `b`.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Rebuild and rerun AddressSanitizer and libFuzzer on YuvRgbFuzzTest.Convert to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirm the overflow no longer reproduces.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Run the full test suite to verify no regressions.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBy following this targeted approach, we eliminate the stack buffer overflow while [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving the intent and precision of the “spill” algorithm in the slow‐path [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconverter.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
